+// Call Vertex AI Gemini
+async function callGemini(accessToken, prompt, imageBase64) {
+  const projectID = 'project-51cbdab8-586c-4f77-94c';
+  const location = 'asia-southeast1';
+  
+  // Try Gemini models in order of preference
+  const models = [
+    'gemini-2.5-flash-preview-05-20',
+    'gemini-2.0-flash-001',
+    'gemini-1.5-flash-002'
+  ];
+  
+  let lastError = null;
+  
+  for (const model of models) {
+    try {
+      const endpoint = `https://${location}-aiplatform.googleapis.com/v1/projects/${projectID}/locations/${location}/publishers/google/models/${model}:generateContent`;
+      
+      const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
+        method: 'POST',
+        headers: {
+          'Authorization': `Bearer ${accessToken}`,
+          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
+        },
+        body: JSON.stringify({
+          contents: [{
+            role: 'user',
+            parts: [
+              { text: prompt },
+              { inlineData: { mimeType: 'image/jpeg', data: imageBase64 } }
+            ]
+          }],
+          generationConfig: {
+            temperature: 0.3,
+            maxOutputTokens: 500
+          }
+        })
+      });
+      
+      if (response.ok) {
+        const data = await response.json();
+        const text = data.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text;
+        if (text) {
+          console.log(`Success with model: ${model}`);
+          return { text, model };
+        }
+      } else {
+        const errText = await response.text();
+        lastError = `${model}: ${response.status} - ${errText.substring(0, 200)}`;
+        console.log(lastError);
+      }
+    } catch (err) {
+      lastError = `${model}: ${err.message}`;
+      console.log(lastError);
+    }
+  }
+  
+  throw new Error(lastError || 'All Gemini models failed');
+}

+// === EDGE-NATIVE GOOGLE CLOUD AUTHENTICATION ENGINE ===
+// Generates short-lived OAuth2 tokens without requiring Node.js libraries
+async function getGoogleAuthToken() {
+  const saJson = process.env.GCP_SERVICE_ACCOUNT;
+  if (!saJson) throw new Error("GCP_SERVICE_ACCOUNT environment variable is missing in Vercel.");
+  const sa = JSON.parse(saJson);
+
+  const header = { alg: 'RS256', typ: 'JWT' };
+  const iat = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
+  const exp = iat + 3600; // Token valid for 1 hour
+  const payload = {
+    iss: sa.client_email,
+    aud: 'https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token',
+    scope: 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/cloud-platform',
+    iat, exp
+  };
+
+  const base64url = (str) => btoa(str).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=+$/, '');
+  const unsignedData = `${base64url(JSON.stringify(header))}.${base64url(JSON.stringify(payload))}`;
+
+  // Convert PEM private key to ArrayBuffer for Web Crypto
+  const b64Lines = sa.private_key.replace(/-----BEGIN PRIVATE KEY-----/g, '').replace(/-----END PRIVATE KEY-----/g, '').replace(/\s+/g, '');
+  const b64Decoded = atob(b64Lines);
+  const keyBuffer = new Uint8Array(b64Decoded.length);
+  for (let i = 0; i < b64Decoded.length; i++) keyBuffer[i] = b64Decoded.charCodeAt(i);
+
+  const cryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
+    'pkcs8', keyBuffer.buffer, { name: 'RSASSA-PKCS1-v1_5', hash: 'SHA-256' }, false, ['sign']
+  );
+
+  const signature = await crypto.subtle.sign('RSASSA-PKCS1-v1_5', cryptoKey, new TextEncoder().encode(unsignedData));
+  const encodedSignature = btoa(String.fromCharCode(...new Uint8Array(signature))).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=+$/, '');
+  const jwt = `${unsignedData}.${encodedSignature}`;
+
+  // Exchange signed JWT for an access token
+  const tokenRes = await fetch('https://oauth2.googleapis.com/token', {
+    method: 'POST',
+    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' },
+    body: `grant_type=urn%3Aietf%3Aparams%3Aoauth%3Agrant-type%3Ajwt-bearer&assertion=${jwt}`
+  });
+
+  const tokenData = await tokenRes.json();
+  if (!tokenData.access_token) throw new Error("Failed to exchange JWT for Access Token.");
+  return tokenData.access_token;
+}
+

+function handleBgUpload(e) {

+// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
+// THE SPATIAL ENGINE (Recognition & Grounding)
+// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
+function applyEffect(canvas, charImg, variation = {}) {
+  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { willReadFrequently: true });
+  const settings = { ...S, ...variation };
+  const w = canvas.parentElement.clientWidth, h = canvas.parentElement.clientHeight;
+  canvas.width = w; canvas.height = h;
+
+  // 1. DYNAMIC GROUND CALCULATIONS
+  const horizonY = h * S.world.horizonY;
+  const floorHeight = h - horizonY;
+  
+  // Pivot character feet on the predicted ground plane (at 90% of floor depth)
+  const feetY = horizonY + (floorHeight * 0.9);
+  const feetX = w / 2;
 
-  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response(null, { status: 200, headers });
+  // Movement Logic
+  let bgScale = 1.0;
+  let charScaleAdjust = 1.0;
+  let verticalShift = 0;
+  let horizontalShift = 0;
+
+  if (variation.type === 'end') {
+    const intensity = (S.zoom - 1);
+    switch(settings.movement) {
+      case 'Dolly Push In':
+        bgScale = 1.15;
+        charScaleAdjust = 1.4;
+        break;
+      case 'Dolly Pull Out':
+        bgScale = 0.85;
+        charScaleAdjust = 0.7;
+        break;
+      case 'Dolly Zoom':
+        bgScale = 1.6; // BG gets big
+        charScaleAdjust = 0.6; // Subject shrinks to compensate
+        break;
+      case 'Tilt Up':
+        verticalShift = h * 0.15; // Camera looks up, everything moves down
+        break;
+      case 'Pan Left':
+        horizontalShift = w * 0.15;
+        break;
+    }
+  }
+
+  ctx.save();
   
-  const apiKey = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY;
-  if (!apiKey) {
-    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ 
-      error: 'API Key Missing',
-      description: 'Cinematic shot of subject isolated from studio, integrated into scene. Professional lighting. Ready for compositing.',
-      analyzed: false
-    }), { status: 200, headers });
+  // 2. RENDER THE "DOME" BACKGROUND (Overscanned)
+  if (S.bgImg) {
+    const bgRatio = S.bgImg.width / S.bgImg.height;
+    const drawH = h * S.world.fov * bgScale;
+    const drawW = drawH * bgRatio;
+    
+    ctx.translate(feetX + horizontalShift, feetY + verticalShift);
+    ctx.drawImage(S.bgImg, -drawW/2, -drawH * 0.85, drawW, drawH);
+    ctx.resetTransform();
+  } else {
+    ctx.fillStyle = '#0a0a0c'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
   }
 
+  // 3. UNIVERSAL CHARACTER GROUNDING
+  const charRatio = charImg.width / charImg.height;
+  const baseCharH = h * 0.75 * charScaleAdjust;
+  const baseCharW = baseCharH * charRatio;
+
+  // Extract char and remove studio gray
+  const temp = document.createElement('canvas');
+  temp.width = w; temp.height = h;
+  const tCtx = temp.getContext('2d');
+  
+  // Place character so feet are at (feetX, feetY)
+  tCtx.drawImage(charImg, feetX - baseCharW/2, feetY - baseCharH, baseCharW, baseCharH);
+  
+  const imageData = tCtx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h);
+  const pixels = imageData.data;
+  for (let i = 0; i < pixels.length; i += 4) {
+    const r = pixels[i], g = pixels[i+1], b = pixels[i+2];
+    // STUDIO GRAY SUPPRESSION (Optimized for Xiaomi)
+    if (Math.abs(r-g) < 15 && Math.abs(r-b) < 15 && r > 60 && r < 200) {
+      pixels[i+3] = 0; 
+    }
+  }
+  tCtx.putImageData(imageData, 0, 0);
+  
+  // Apply final character shadow based on predicted ground
+  ctx.save();
+  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.4;
+  ctx.filter = 'blur(10px)';
+  ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
+  ctx.beginPath();
+  ctx.ellipse(feetX, feetY, baseCharW * 0.4, 10, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
+  ctx.fill();
+  ctx.restore();
+
+  ctx.drawImage(temp, 0, 0);
+  ctx.restore();
+}

+  if (request.method !== 'POST') {
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Method not allowed' }), { status: 405, headers });
+  }
+
+  // 4. Validate API Key from Vercel Environment Variables
   const apiKey = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY;
   if (!apiKey) {
-    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY is missing' }), { status: 500, headers });
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'GEMINI_API_KEY is missing in Vercel settings' }), { status: 500, headers });
   }
 
   try {
     const { imageBase64, cinematographyContext } = await request.json();
 
     if (!imageBase64) {
-      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Missing image data' }), { status: 400, headers });
+      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'No image data received' }), { status: 400, headers });
     }
 
-    // CRITICAL FIX: Ensure strictly raw Base64 string is extracted
-    const cleanBase64 = imageBase64.split(',')[1] || imageBase64;
-
-    const prompt = `ACT AS: A-CAM Senior DP. Analyze subject. 
-      IGNORE studio background, lights, and floor. 
-      PLACE subject into: ${cinematographyContext}.
-      OUTPUT: Single paragraph cinematography prompt starting with 'Cinematic shot of [Subject] isolated from studio and integrated into...'`;
-
-   // Inside analyze.js, update the fetch URL to v1 stable
-const response = await fetch(
-  `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`,
-  {
-    method: 'POST',
-    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
-    body: JSON.stringify({
-      contents: [{
-        parts: [
-          { text: prompt },
-          { inline_data: { mime_type: 'image/jpeg', data: imageBase64.split(',')[1] } }
-        ]
-      }]
-    })
-  }
-);
+    // 5. Clean the Base64 string (Google requires ONLY the raw data, no "data:image/jpeg..." prefix)
+    const cleanBase64 = imageBase64.includes(',') ? imageBase64.split(',')[1] : imageBase64;
+
+    // 6. The "Director" Prompt - This is the logic that "removes" your background
+    const prompt = `
+      ACT AS: A-CAM Senior Director of Photography.
+      TASK: Analyze the character (MiguelMX) and prepare a technical prompt for a video model.
+      
+      CRITICAL INSTRUCTIONS:
+      1. BACKGROUND SUPPRESSION: The subject is in a gray studio. You MUST ignore all studio elements (lights, backdrops, stands). 
+      2. SUBJECT ISOLATION: Describe the subject as if they are already cut out (alpha channel).
+      3. ENVIRONMENT INTEGRATION: Describe how the subject fits into this specific scene: ${cinematographyContext}.
+      4. LIGHTING: Match the subject's lighting to the target scene's atmosphere.
+
+      OUTPUT: A single technical paragraph starting with "Cinematic shot of [Subject] isolated from studio and integrated into..."
+    `;
+
+    // 7. Call Google Gemini 1.5 Flash via v1beta (Required for this specific model/task combo)
+    const response = await fetch(
+      `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`,
+      {
+        method: 'POST',
+        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
+        body: JSON.stringify({
+          contents: [{
+            parts: [
+              { text: prompt },
+              { inline_data: { mime_type: 'image/jpeg', data: cleanBase64 } }
+            ]
+          }]
+        })
+      }
+    );
 
     const data = await response.json();
 
+    // 8. Handle Google-side errors (Invalid keys, model busy, etc.)
     if (!response.ok) {
-      // If Google returns an error (like invalid key), we catch it here
-      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: data.error?.message || 'Google API Error' }), { status: 500, headers });
+      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ 
+        error: data.error?.message || 'Google API Error',
+        details: data 
+      }), { status: 500, headers });
     }
 
+    // 9. Extract the generated text
     const description = data.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || 'Analysis complete.';
-    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ description, analyzed: true }), { status: 200, headers });
+
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ 
+      description: description,
+      analyzed: true 
+    }), { status: 200, headers });
 
   } catch (error) {
-    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Edge Runtime Error: ' + error.message }), { status: 500, headers });
+    // 10. Catch Edge Runtime crashes (Timeouts or payload issues)
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Edge Function Crash: ' + error.message }), { status: 500, headers });
   }

+// To enable:
+// 1. Add GEMINI_API_KEY to Vercel Environment Variables
+// 2. The frontend will auto-detect and use this endpoint
+
+export const config = {
+  runtime: 'edge',
+};
+
+export default async function handler(request) {
+  // CORS headers
+  const headers = {
+    'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
+    'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
+    'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
+    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
+  };
+
+  if (request.method === 'OPTIONS') {
+    return new Response(null, { status: 200, headers });
+  }
+
+  if (request.method !== 'POST') {
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Method not allowed' }), {
+      status: 405,
+      headers,
+    });
+  }
+
+  const apiKey = process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY;
+  
+  if (!apiKey) {
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ 
+      error: 'API key not configured',
+      fallback: true,
+      description: 'Central subject with professional composition, natural lighting with soft shadows, clean background with appropriate depth separation.'
+    }), {
+      status: 200,
+      headers,
+    });
+  }
+
+  try {
+    const { imageBase64, cinematographyContext } = await request.json();
+
+    if (!imageBase64) {
+      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'No image provided' }), {
+        status: 400,
+        headers,
+      });
+    }
+
+    const prompt = `Analyze this image for cinematic video generation.
+
+Context: ${cinematographyContext || 'General cinematography'}
+
+Describe the scene in 2-3 sentences focusing on:
+1. Subject positioning and composition
+2. Lighting quality and direction
+3. Background elements and depth
+4. Suggested motion that would enhance this frame
+
+Be concise and technical. Optimize for AI video generation prompts.`;
+
+    const response = await fetch(
+      `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-1.5-flash:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`,
+      {
+        method: 'POST',
+        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
+        body: JSON.stringify({
+          contents: [{
+            parts: [
+              { text: prompt },
+              {
+                inline_data: {
+                  mime_type: 'image/jpeg',
+                  data: imageBase64.replace(/^data:image\/\w+;base64,/, '')
+                }
+              }
+            ]
+          }],
+          generationConfig: {
+            temperature: 0.4,
+            maxOutputTokens: 200
+          }
+        })
+      }
+    );
+
+    if (!response.ok) {
+      throw new Error(`Gemini API error: ${response.status}`);
+    }
+
+    const data = await response.json();
+    const description = data.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || 
+      'Professional composition with balanced lighting and clean background.';
+
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ 
+      description,
+      analyzed: true 
+    }), {
+      status: 200,
+      headers,
+    });
+
+  } catch (error) {
+    console.error('Analyze error:', error);
+    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ 
+      error: error.message,
+      fallback: true,
+      description: 'Central subject with professional composition, natural lighting with soft shadows, clean background with appropriate depth separation.'
+    }), {
+      status: 200,
+      headers,
+    });
+  }
+}
